											<div class="menuOptionsArrow"><img src="/assets-v3/images/menu/menuOptionsArrowLeft.png" alt="decorative arrow" /></div>
											<div onClick="BLB.switchShowState('advOptMenu', 'searchDrop');" class="menuOptionsClose"><img src="/assets-v3/images/menu/menuOptionsClose_a.png" alt="Close Advanced Options" /></div>
										</div>
									</div>
								</div>
							</form>

 <a title="Strong's G5590" href="/lexicon/G5590/kjv/tr/0-1/">G5590</a>.</p></div>

								<div class="row">
									<div class="columns small-12" id="lexOut">
										<div class="row">
											<div class="columns small-12 table-styles">
												<div class="lexicon-label expandable expandable-closed" onclick="BLB.Bible.toggleVisibility(this,['outlineBiblical'])">Outline of Biblical Usage <a class="lexpop show-for-medium" rel="lexicon.obuHelp">[?]</a></div>
												<div id="outlineBiblical" class="__hidden"><div>
<ol>
    <li>
        <p>
            life
        </p>
        <ol>
            <li>
                <p>
                    the state of one who is possessed of vitality or is animate
                </p>
            </li>
            <li>
                <p>
                    every living soul
                </p>
            </li>
        </ol>
    </li>
    <li>
        <p>
            life
        </p>
        <ol>
            <li>
                <p>
                    of the absolute fulness of life, both essential and ethical, which belongs to God, and through him both to the hypostatic &quot;logos&quot; and to Christ in whom the &quot;logos&quot; put on human nature
                </p>
            </li>
            <li>
                <p>
                    life real and genuine, a life active and vigorous, devoted to God, blessed, in the portion even in this world of those who put their trust in Christ, but after the resurrection to be consummated by new accessions (among them a more perfect body), and to last for ever.
                </p>
            </li>
        </ol>
    </li>
</ol>

										<div id="lexyText" class="show-hide-ten show-ten">
								
												<div class="thayer-title no-print">
													<span>STRONGS G2222:</span>
													<span>
														<span class="show-hide-ten"></span>
													</span>
												</div>
									    		<span class="lexicon-word"><span class="Gk">ζωή</span></span>, <span class="Gk maroon">ζωῆς</span>, <span class="Gk maroon">ἡ</span> (from <span class="Gk maroon">ζάω</span>, <span class="Gk maroon">ζῶ</span>), the <span class="text-abbreviation">Sept.</span> chiefly for <span class="Hb maroon">חַיִּים</span>; <span class="emphasis">life</span>; <br />
<span class="thbullet-lvl2">1.</span> universally, <span class="emphasis">life,</span> i. e. <span class="emphasis">the state of one who is possessed of vitality or is animate</span>: <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/1pe/3/10/s_1154010" id="si_1">1 Peter 3:10</a> (on which see <span class="thayer-ref"><span class="Gk maroon">ἀγαπάω</span></span>); <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/heb/7/3/s_1140003" id="si_2">Hebrews 7:3</a>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/heb/7/16/s_1140016" id="si_3">16</a>; <span class="Gk maroon">αὐτός</span> (<span class="Gk maroon">ὁ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">Θεός</span>) <span class="Gk maroon">διδούς</span> <span class="Gk maroon">πᾶσιν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωήν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">καί</span> <span class="Gk maroon">πνοήν</span>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/act/17/25/s_1035025" id="si_4">Acts 17:25</a>; <span class="Gk maroon">πνεῦμα</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωῆς</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ἐκ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">τοῦ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">Θεοῦ</span>, the vital spirit, the breath of (i. e. imparting) life, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/rev/11/11/s_1178011" id="si_5">Revelation 11:11</a> (<a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/eze/37/5/s_839005" id="si_6">Ezekiel 37:5</a>); <span class="Gk maroon">πᾶσα</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ψυχή</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωῆς</span>, genitive of possess, <span class="emphasis">every living soul,</span> <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/rev/16/3/s_1183003" id="si_7">Revelation 16:3</a> <span class="text-abbreviation">G</span> <span class="text-abbreviation">L</span> <span class="text-abbreviation">T</span> <span class="text-abbreviation">Tr</span> text <span class="text-abbreviation">WH</span>; spoken of earthly life: <span class="Gk maroon">ἡ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωή</span> <span class="Gk maroon">τίνος</span>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/luk/12/15/s_985015" id="si_8">Luke 12:15</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/act/8/33/s_1026033" id="si_9">Acts 8:33</a> (see <span class="thayer-ref"><span class="Gk maroon">αἴρω</span></span>, 3 h.); <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jas/4/14/s_1150014" id="si_10">James 4:14</a>; <span class="Gk maroon">ἐν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">τῇ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωή</span> <span class="Gk maroon">σου</span>, whilst thou wast living on earth, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/luk/16/25/s_989025" id="si_11">Luke 16:25</a> (<span class="Gk maroon">ἐν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">τῇ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωή</span> <span class="Gk maroon">αὐτοῦ</span>, Sir. 30:5 Sir. 50:1); <span class="Gk maroon">ἐν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">τῇ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωή</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ταύτῃ</span>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/1co/15/19/s_1077019" id="si_12">1 Corinthians 15:19</a>; <span class="Gk maroon">πᾶσαι</span> <span class="Gk maroon">αἱ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ἡμέραι</span> <span class="Gk maroon">τῆς</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωῆς</span> <span class="Gk maroon">τίνος</span>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/luk/1/75/s_974075" id="si_13">Luke 1:75</a> <span class="text-abbreviation">Rec.</span> (<a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/gen/3/14/s_3014" id="si_14">Genesis 3:14</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/psa/127/5/s_605005" id="si_15">Psalm 127:5</a> (<a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/psa/128/5/s_606005" id="si_16">Ps. 128:5</a>); Sir. 22:12 (10)). <span class="Gk maroon">ἐπαγγελία</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωῆς</span> <span class="Gk maroon">τῆς</span> <span class="Gk maroon">νῦν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">καί</span> <span class="Gk maroon">τῆς</span> <span class="Gk maroon">μελλούσης</span>, a promise looking to the present and the future life, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/1ti/4/8/s_1123008" id="si_17">1 Timothy 4:8</a>; <span class="Gk maroon">ζωή</span> and <span class="Gk maroon">θάνατος</span> are contrasted in <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/rom/8/38/s_1054038" id="si_18">Romans 8:38</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/1co/3/22/s_1065022" id="si_19">1 Corinthians 3:22</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/phl/1/20/s_1104020" id="si_20">Philippians 1:20</a>; of a life preserved in the midst of perils, with a suggestion of vigor, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/2co/4/12/s_1082012" id="si_21">2 Corinthians 4:12</a> (the life of Paul is meant here, which exerts a saving power on the Corinthians by his discharge of his apostolic duties); of the life of persons raised from the dead: <span class="Gk maroon">ἐν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">καινότητι</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωῆς</span>, figuratively spoken of a new mode of life, dedicated to God, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/rom/6/4/s_1052004" id="si_22">Romans 6:4</a>; of the life of Jesus after his resurrection, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/act/2/28/s_1020028" id="si_23">Acts 2:28</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/rom/5/10/s_1051010" id="si_24">Romans 5:10</a>; of the same, with the added notion of vigor, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/2co/4/10/s_1082010" id="si_25">2 Corinthians 4:10f</a>. <br />
<span class="thbullet-lvl2">2.</span> used emphatically, <br />
<span class="thbullet-lvl3">a.</span> <span class="emphasis">of the absolute fullness of life, both essential and ethical, which belongs to God, and through him both to the hypostatic</span> <span class="Gk maroon">λόγος</span> <span class="emphasis">and to Christ</span> in whom the <span class="Gk maroon">λόγος</span> put on human nature: <span class="Gk maroon">ὥσπερ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ὁ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">πατήρ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ἔχει</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωήν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ἐν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ἑαυτῷ</span>, <span class="Gk maroon">οὕτως</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ἔδωκεν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">καί</span> <span class="Gk maroon">τῷ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">υἱῷ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωήν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ἔχειν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ἐν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ἑαυτῷ</span>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/5/26/s_1002026" id="si_26">John 5:26</a>; <span class="Gk maroon">ἐν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">αὐτῷ</span> (namely, <span class="Gk maroon">τῷ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">λόγῳ</span>) <span class="Gk maroon">ζωή</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ἦν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">καί</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ἡ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωή</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ἦν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">τό</span> <span class="Gk maroon">φῶς</span> <span class="Gk maroon">τῶν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ἀνθρώπων</span>, in him life was (comprehended), and the life (transfused from the Logos into created natures) was the light (i. e. the intelligence) of men (because the life of men is self-conscious, and thus a fountain of intelligence springs up), <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/1/4/s_998004" id="si_27">John 1:4</a>; <span class="Gk maroon">ὁ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">λόγος</span> <span class="Gk maroon">τῆς</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωῆς</span>, the Logos having life in itself and communicating it to others, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/1jo/1/1/s_1160001" id="si_28">1 John 1:1</a>; <span class="Gk maroon">ἡ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωή</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ἐφανερώθη</span>, was manifested in Christ, clothed in flesh, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/1jo/1/2/s_1160002" id="si_29">1 John 1:2</a>. From this divine fountain of life flows forth that life which is next to be defined: viz. <br />
<span class="thbullet-lvl3">b.</span> <span class="emphasis">life real and genuine,</span> <span class="emphasis">vita quae sola vita nominanda</span> (<span class="author-abbreviation">Cicero</span>, de sen. 21, 77), <span class="emphasis">a life active and vigorous, devoted to God, blessed, the portion even in this world of those who put their trust in Christ, but after the resurrection to be consummated by new accessions (among them a more perfect body), and to last forever</span> (the writers of the O. T. have anticipated the conception, in their way, by employing <span class="Hb maroon">חַיִּים</span> to denote a happy life and every kind of blessing: <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/deu/30/15/s_183015" id="si_30">Deuteronomy 30:15</a>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/deu/30/19/s_183019" id="si_31">19</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/mal/2/5/s_927005" id="si_32">Malachi 2:5</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/psa/33/13/s_511013" id="si_33">Psalm 33:13</a> (<a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/psa/34/13/s_512013" id="si_34">Ps. 34:13</a>) 13; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/pro/8/35/s_636035" id="si_35">Proverbs 8:35</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/pro/12/28/s_640028" id="si_36">Proverbs 12:28</a>, etc.): <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/6/51/s_1003051" id="si_37">John 6:51</a>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/6/63/s_1003063" id="si_38">63</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/14/6/s_1011006" id="si_39">John 14:6</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/rom/7/10/s_1053010" id="si_40">Romans 7:10</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/rom/8/6/s_1054006" id="si_41">Romans 8:6</a>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/rom/8/10/s_1054010" id="si_42">10</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/2co/2/16/s_1080016" id="si_43">2 Corinthians 2:16</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/phl/2/16/s_1105016" id="si_44">Philippians 2:16</a>; (<a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/col/3/4/s_1110004" id="si_45">Colossians 3:4</a>); <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/2pe/1/3/s_1157003" id="si_46">2 Peter 1:3</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/1jo/5/11/s_1164011" id="si_47">1 John 5:11</a>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/1jo/5/16/s_1164016" id="si_48">16</a>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/1jo/5/20/s_1164020" id="si_49">20</a>; with the addition of <span class="Gk maroon">τοῦ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">Θεοῦ</span>, supplied by God (<span class="author-abbreviation">Winer</span>&#39;s Grammar, 186 (175)), <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/eph/4/18/s_1101018" id="si_50">Ephesians 4:18</a>; <span class="Gk maroon">ἡ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ἐν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">Χριστῷ</span>, to be obtained in fellowship with Christ, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/2ti/1/1/s_1126001" id="si_51">2 Timothy 1:1</a>; <span class="Gk maroon">μεταβεβηκέναι</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ἐκ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">τοῦ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">θανάτου</span> <span class="Gk maroon">εἰς</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωήν</span>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/5/24/s_1002024" id="si_52">John 5:24</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/1jo/3/14/s_1162014" id="si_53">1 John 3:14</a>; <span class="Gk maroon">ὄψεσθαί</span> <span class="Gk maroon">τήν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωήν</span>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/3/36/s_1000036" id="si_54">John 3:36</a>; <span class="Gk maroon">ἔχειν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωήν</span>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/5/40/s_1002040" id="si_55">John 5:40</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/10/10/s_1007010" id="si_56">John 10:10</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/1jo/5/12/s_1164012" id="si_57">1 John 5:12</a>; with <span class="Gk maroon">ἐν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ἑαυτῷ</span> (or <span class="Gk maroon">ἑαυτοῖς</span>) added, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/5/26/s_1002026" id="si_58">John 5:26</a>; (<a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/6/53/s_1003053" id="si_59">John 6:53</a>); <span class="Gk maroon">διδόναι</span>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/6/33/s_1003033" id="si_60">John 6:33</a>; <span class="Gk maroon">χάρις</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωῆς</span>, the grace of God evident in the life obtained, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/1pe/3/7/s_1154007" id="si_61">1 Peter 3:7</a>; <span class="Gk maroon">τό</span> <span class="Gk maroon">πνεῦμα</span> <span class="Gk maroon">τῆς</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωῆς</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ἐν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">Χριστῷ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">Ἰησοῦ</span>, the Spirit, the repository and imparter of life, and which is received by those united to Christ, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/rom/8/2/s_1054002" id="si_62">Romans 8:2</a>; <span class="Gk maroon">ὁ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ἄρτος</span> <span class="Gk maroon">τῆς</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωῆς</span> (see <span class="thayer-ref"><span class="Gk maroon">ἄρτος</span></span>, at the end), <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/6/35/s_1003035" id="si_63">John 6:35</a>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/6/48/s_1003048" id="si_64">48</a>; <span class="Gk maroon">τό</span> <span class="Gk maroon">φῶς</span> <span class="Gk maroon">τῆς</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζοης</span>, the light illumined by which one arrives at life, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/8/12/s_1005012" id="si_65">John 8:12</a>. more fully <span class="Gk maroon">ζωή</span> <span class="Gk maroon">αἰώνιος</span> and <span class="Gk maroon">ἡ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωή</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ἡ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">αἰώνιος</span> ((cf. <span class="author-abbreviation">Buttmann</span>, 90 (79)); see below): <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/4/36/s_1001036" id="si_66">John 4:36</a>; (<a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/12/50/s_1009050" id="si_67">John 12:50</a>); <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/17/3/s_1014003" id="si_68">John 17:3</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/1jo/1/2/s_1160002" id="si_69">1 John 1:2</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/1jo/2/25/s_1161025" id="si_70">1 John 2:25</a>; (<span class="Gk maroon">ῤήματα</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωῆς</span> <span class="Gk maroon">αἰωνίου</span>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/6/68/s_1003068" id="si_71">John 6:68</a>); <span class="Gk maroon">εἰς</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωήν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">αἰώνιον</span>, unto the attainment of eternal life (cf. <span class="thayer-ref"><span class="Gk maroon">εἰς</span></span>, B. II. 3 c. <span class="Gk maroon">δ</span>., p. 185a), <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/4/14/s_1001014" id="si_72">John 4:14</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/6/27/s_1003027" id="si_73">John 6:27</a>; <span class="Gk maroon">διδόναι</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωήν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">αἰώνιον</span>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/10/28/s_1007028" id="si_74">John 10:28</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/17/2/s_1014002" id="si_75">John 17:2</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/1jo/5/11/s_1164011" id="si_76">1 John 5:11</a>; <span class="Gk maroon">ἔχειν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωήν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">αἰώνιον</span>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/3/15/s_1000015" id="si_77">John 3:15</a> (and <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/3/16/s_1000016" id="si_78">John 3:16</a>) (opposed to <span class="Gk maroon">ἀπολλυσθαι</span>), <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/3/36/s_1000036" id="si_79">John 3:36</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/5/24/s_1002024" id="si_80">John 5:24</a>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/5/39/s_1002039" id="si_81">39</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/6/40/s_1003040" id="si_82">John 6:40</a>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/6/47/s_1003047" id="si_83">47</a>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/6/54/s_1003054" id="si_84">54</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/20/31/s_1017031" id="si_85">John 20:31</a> <span class="text-abbreviation">L</span> brackets; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/1jo/5/13/s_1164013" id="si_86">1 John 5:13</a>; <span class="Gk maroon">οὐκ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ἔχειν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωήν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">αἰώνιον</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ἐν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ἑαυτῷ</span>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/1jo/3/15/s_1162015" id="si_87">1 John 3:15</a>; (in Enoch 15:4,6 the wicked angels are said before their fall to have been <span class="emphasis">spiritual</span> and <span class="emphasis">partakers of eternal and immortal life</span>). <span class="Gk maroon">ζωή</span> and <span class="Gk maroon">ἡ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωή</span>, without epithet, are used of the blessing of <span class="emphasis">real life after the resurrection,</span> in <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/mat/7/14/s_936014" id="si_88">Matthew 7:14</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/11/25/s_1008025" id="si_89">John 11:25</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/act/3/15/s_1021015" id="si_90">Acts 3:15</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/act/5/20/s_1023020" id="si_91">Acts 5:20</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/act/11/18/s_1029018" id="si_92">Acts 11:18</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/rom/5/17/s_1051017" id="si_93">Romans 5:17</a>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/rom/5/18/s_1051018" id="si_94">18</a> (on which see <span class="thayer-ref"><span class="Gk maroon">δικαίωσις</span></span>, at the end); <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/2co/5/4/s_1083004" id="si_95">2 Corinthians 5:4</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/col/3/3/s_1110003" id="si_96">Colossians 3:3</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/2ti/1/10/s_1126010" id="si_97">2 Timothy 1:10</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/tit/1/2/s_1130002" id="si_98">Titus 1:2</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/tit/3/7/s_1132007" id="si_99">Titus 3:7</a>; <span class="Gk maroon">ζωή</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ἐκ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">νεκρῶν</span>, life breaking forth from the abode of the dead, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/rom/11/15/s_1057015" id="si_100">Romans 11:15</a>; <span class="Gk maroon">εἰσελθεῖν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">εἰς</span> <span class="Gk maroon">τήν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωήν</span>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/mat/18/8/s_947008" id="si_101">Matthew 18:8</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/mat/19/17/s_948017" id="si_102">Matthew 19:17</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/mar/9/43/s_966043" id="si_103">Mark 9:43</a>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/mar/9/45/s_966045" id="si_104">45</a>; <span class="Gk maroon">ἀνάστασις</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωῆς</span> equivalent to <span class="Gk maroon">εἰς</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωήν</span> (2 Macc. 7:14), <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/5/29/s_1002029" id="si_105">John 5:29</a> (on the genitive, cf. <span class="author-abbreviation">Winer</span>&#39;s Grammar, 188 (177)); <span class="Gk maroon">στέφανος</span> <span class="Gk maroon">τῆς</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωῆς</span> equivalent to <span class="Gk maroon">ἡ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωή</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ὡς</span> <span class="Gk maroon">στέφανος</span>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jas/1/12/s_1147012" id="si_106">James 1:12</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/rev/2/10/s_1169010" id="si_107">Revelation 2:10</a>; <span class="Gk maroon">ξύλον</span> <span class="Gk maroon">τῆς</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωῆς</span>, the tree whose fruit gives and maintains eternal life, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/rev/2/7/s_1169007" id="si_108">Revelation 2:7</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/rev/22/2/s_1189002" id="si_109">Revelation 22:2</a>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/rev/22/14/s_1189014" id="si_110">14</a>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/rev/22/19/s_1189019" id="si_111">19</a> (<span class="text-abbreviation">G</span> <span class="text-abbreviation">L</span> <span class="text-abbreviation">T</span> <span class="text-abbreviation">Tr</span> <span class="text-abbreviation">WH</span>) (cf. <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/gen/2/9/s_2009" id="si_112">Genesis 2:9</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/pro/3/18/s_631018" id="si_113">Proverbs 3:18</a>; <span class="Gk maroon">δένδρον</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωῆς</span>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/pro/11/30/s_639030" id="si_114">Proverbs 11:30</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/pro/13/12/s_641012" id="si_115">Proverbs 13:12</a>); cf. Bleek, Vorless. üb. d. Apokalypse, p. 174f; <span class="Gk maroon">ὕδωρ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωῆς</span>, water the use of which serves to maintain eternal life, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/rev/21/6/s_1188006" id="si_116">Revelation 21:6</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/rev/22/1/s_1189001" id="si_117">Revelation 22:1</a>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/rev/22/17/s_1189017" id="si_118">17</a>; in the same sense <span class="Gk maroon">ζωῆς</span> <span class="Gk maroon">πηγαί</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ὑδάτων</span>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/rev/7/17/s_1174017" id="si_119">Revelation 7:17</a> <span class="text-abbreviation">G</span> <span class="text-abbreviation">L</span> <span class="text-abbreviation">T</span> <span class="text-abbreviation">Tr</span> <span class="text-abbreviation">WH</span>; <span class="Gk maroon">ἡ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">βίβλος</span> and <span class="Gk maroon">τό</span> <span class="Gk maroon">βιβλίον</span> <span class="Gk maroon">τῆς</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωῆς</span>, the book in which the names of those are recorded to whom eternal life has been decreed: <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/phl/4/3/s_1107003" id="si_120">Philippians 4:3</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/rev/3/5/s_1170005" id="si_121">Revelation 3:5</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/rev/13/8/s_1180008" id="si_122">Revelation 13:8</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/rev/17/8/s_1184008" id="si_123">Revelation 17:8</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/rev/20/12/s_1187012" id="si_124">Revelation 20:12</a>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/rev/20/15/s_1187015" id="si_125">15</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/rev/21/27/s_1188027" id="si_126">Revelation 21:27</a>; (<a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/rev/22/19/s_1189019" id="si_127">Revelation 22:19</a> <span class="text-abbreviation">Rec.</span>; cf. <span class="author-abbreviation">Lightfoot</span> on Philippians, the passage cited), more fully <span class="Gk maroon">ἡ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ὄντως</span> (<span class="text-abbreviation">Rec.</span> <span class="Gk maroon">αἰώνιος</span>) <span class="Gk maroon">ζωή</span>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/1ti/6/19/s_1125019" id="si_128">1 Timothy 6:19</a>; <span class="Gk maroon">ζωή</span> <span class="Gk maroon">αἰώνιος</span> (cf. above) (<span class="author-abbreviation">Justin Martyr</span>, de resurr. i., p. 588 c. <span class="Gk maroon">ὁ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">λόγος</span>... <span class="Gk maroon">διδούς</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ἡμῖν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ἐν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ἑαυτῷ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">τήν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ἐκ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">νεκρῶν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ἀνάστασιν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">καί</span> <span class="Gk maroon">τήν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">μετά</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ταῦτα</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωήν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">αἰώνιον</span>), <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/mat/25/46/s_954046" id="si_129">Matthew 25:46</a> (opposed to <span class="Gk maroon">κόλασις</span> <span class="Gk maroon">αἰώνιος</span>); <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/act/13/46/s_1031046" id="si_130">Acts 13:46</a>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/act/13/48/s_1031048" id="si_131">48</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/rom/2/7/s_1048007" id="si_132">Romans 2:7</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/rom/6/22/s_1052022" id="si_133">Romans 6:22</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/gal/6/8/s_1097008" id="si_134">Galatians 6:8</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/1ti/6/12/s_1125012" id="si_135">1 Timothy 6:12</a>; after <span class="Gk maroon">ἐν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">τῷ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">αἰῶνι</span> <span class="Gk maroon">τῷ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ἐρχομένῳ</span>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/mar/10/30/s_967030" id="si_136">Mark 10:30</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/luk/18/30/s_991030" id="si_137">Luke 18:30</a>; <span class="Gk maroon">ἔχειν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωήν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">αἰώνιον</span> <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/mat/19/16/s_948016" id="si_138">Matthew 19:16</a>; <span class="Gk maroon">κληρονομεῖν</span>, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/mat/19/29/s_948029" id="si_139">Matthew 19:29</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/mar/10/17/s_967017" id="si_140">Mark 10:17</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/luk/10/25/s_983025" id="si_141">Luke 10:25</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/luk/18/18/s_991018" id="si_142">Luke 18:18</a>; <span class="Gk maroon">εἰς</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωήν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">αἰώνιον</span>, unto the attainment of life eternal, <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/12/25/s_1009025" id="si_143">John 12:25</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/rom/5/21/s_1051021" id="si_144">Romans 5:21</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/1ti/1/16/s_1120016" id="si_145">1 Timothy 1:16</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jde/1/21/s_1167021" id="si_146">Jude 1:21</a> (<a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/dan/12/2/s_862002" id="si_147">Daniel 12:2</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/dan/4/1-37/s_854001" id="si_148">4</a> Macc. 15:2; <span class="Gk maroon">ἀενναος</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωή</span>, 2 Macc. 7:36; <span class="Gk maroon">ἀΐδιος</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωή</span>, <span class="author-abbreviation">Ignatius</span> ad Eph. 19 [ET]). Cf. Köstlin, Lehrbegriff des Ev. Johann. etc., pp. 234ff, 338ff; Reuss, Johann. Theologie (in Beiträge zu d. theol. Wissenschaften, vol. i.), p. 76ff (cf. his Hist. de la Theol. Chret., book vii., chapter xiv.); <span class="author-abbreviation">Lipsius</span>, Paulin. Rechtfertigungslehre, pp. 152ff 185f; Güder in <span class="author-abbreviation">Herzog</span> viii. 254 (2nd edition, 509ff); B. B. Brückner, De notione vocis <span class="Gk maroon">ζωή</span> in N. T. <span class="author-abbreviation">Lipsius</span> 1858; Huther, d. Bedeut. d. Begriffe <span class="Gk maroon">ζωή</span> u. <span class="Gk maroon">πιστεύειν</span> im N. T., in the Jahrbb. f. deutsche Theol. 1872, p. 1ff (For the relations of the term to heathen conceptions cf. G. Teichmüller, <span class="author-abbreviation">Aristotle</span>, Forsch. iii., p. 127ff) Some, as Bretschneider, Wahl, Wilke, especially Käuffer (in his book De biblica <span class="Gk maroon">ζωῆς</span> <span class="Gk maroon">αἰωνίου</span> notione. Dresd. 1838); <em>Westcott</em>, Epp. of St. John, p. 204 sqq., maintain that <span class="Gk maroon">ζωή</span> <span class="Gk maroon">αἰώνιος</span> everywhere even in John&#39;s writings refers to <span class="emphasis">life after the resurrection</span>; but in this way they are compelled not only to assume a prophetic use of the perfect in the saying <span class="Gk maroon">ἐκ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">τοῦ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">θανάτου</span> <span class="Gk maroon">μεταβεβηκέναι</span> <span class="Gk maroon">εἰς</span> <span class="Gk maroon">τήν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωήν</span> (<a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/jhn/5/24/s_1002024" id="si_149">John 5:24</a>; <a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/1jo/3/14/s_1162014" id="si_150">1 John 3:14</a>), but also to interpret the common phrase <span class="Gk maroon">ἔχει</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ζωήν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">αἰώνιον</span> as meaning <span class="emphasis">he has eternal life as his certain portion though as yet only in hope,</span> as well as to explain <span class="Gk maroon">ζωήν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">αἰώνιον</span> <span class="Gk maroon">οὐκ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ἔχειν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ἐν</span> <span class="Gk maroon">ἑαυτῷ</span> <span class="Gk maroon">μένουσαν</span> (<a class="nowrap" href="/kjv/1jo/3/15/s_1162015" id="si_151">1 John 3:15</a>) of <span class="emphasis">the hope</span> of eternal life. (Synonym: see <span class="thayer-ref"><span class="Gk maroon">βίος</span></span>, at the end.)
